In MySQL: CREATE DATABASE company_db;

In PostgreSQL: CREATE DATABASE sales_data;

In SQL Server: using GUI tools to create a new database via "New Database‚Ä¶" dialog ^nS47VkJx

DBMS invocation (command or interface)

Database naming and option specification (encoding, collation, owner)

System resource allocation (disk, memory, metadata structures)

Initialization of empty schema structure ^XhNhYk5T

Attempting to create a database with a duplicate name

Lacking sufficient user privileges to execute CREATE DATABASE

Omitting required configuration parameters such as encoding or owner in systems that enforce them ^yYBTV86D

Database creation vs. schema creation: the database defines the overall container, while a schema defines logical groupings inside it.

Database creation vs. table creation: tables are subordinate objects defined after the database exists. ^cFCpKJm0

In MySQL, creating a database involves issuing the CREATE DATABASE statement followed by a valid database name. This command initializes a new logical container to store, organize, and manage related tables and database objects. The database name must conform to identifier rules (e.g., no reserved words, limited to alphanumeric characters and underscores, must start with a letter). Additional optional clauses like DEFAULT CHARACTER SET and DEFAULT COLLATE can be appended to specify encoding and collation preferences. ^DK5y3H8P
